    32 type PresetKey = 'today' | 'yesterday' | 'week' | 'month' | 'year' | 'custom';
    33 
    34 function toDateStr(d: Date) { return d.toISOString().split('T')[0]; }
    35 
    36 function getPresetRange(key: PresetKey): { from: string; to: string } {
    37   const now = new Date();
    38   const today = toDateStr(now);
    39   if (key === 'today') return { from: today, to: today };
    40   if (key === 'yesterday') {
    41     const y = new Date(now); y.setDate(now.getDate() - 1); const ys = toDateStr(y);
    42     return { from: ys, to: ys };
    43   }
    44   if (key === 'week') {
    45     const w = new Date(now); w.setDate(now.getDate() - 6);
    46     return { from: toDateStr(w), to: today };
    47   }
    48   if (key === 'month') {
    49     return { from: `${now.getFullYear()}-${String(now.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-01`, to: today };
    50   }
    51   if (key === 'year') {
    52     return { from: `${now.getFullYear()}-01-01`, to: today };
    53   }
    54   return { from: today, to: today };
    55 }

    58 function buildChartData(txArr: any[], from: string, to: string): ChartPoint[] {

    60   const end = new Date(`${to}T00:00:00`);

    71         s + (Array.isArray(t.items) ? t.items : []).reduce((si: number, i: any) => si + ((i.unit_price - i.cost) * i.quantity), 0), 0);

   143 export default function RolesPage() {
   144   const { profile } = useAuth();
   145   const [roles, setRoles] = useState<Role[]>([]);
   146   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
   147   const [editingRole, setEditingRole] = useState<Role | null>(null);
   148   const [isCreateOpen, setIsCreateOpen] = useState(false);

   150   const [userCounts, setUserCounts] = useState<Record<string, number>>({});
   151   const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('roles');
   152 
   153   useEffect(() => { loadRoles(); }, []);

   155   const loadRoles = async () => {
   156     setLoading(true);
   157     const { data } = await supabase
   158       .from('roles')
   159       .select('*')
   160       .order('sort_order');
   161     setRoles(Array.isArray(data) ? data : []);
   162

   164     const { data: profileData } = await supabase
   165       .from('profiles')
   166       .select('role_id')
   167       .not('role_id', 'is', null);
   168     const counts: Record<string, number> = {};
   169     (profileData || []).forEach((p: { role_id: string }) => {
   170       if (p.role_id) counts[p.role_id] = (counts[p.role_id] || 0) + 1;
   171     });
   172     setUserCounts(counts);
   173     setLoading(false);
   174   };

   237     toast.success('ลบยศเรียบร้อย');
   238     setDeleteTarget(null);
   239     loadRoles();
   240   };

    81 // ============ Main Component ============
    82 export default function FraudMonitorPage() {
    83   const { profile } = useAuth();
    84   const [tab, setTab] = useState('alerts');
    85   const [alerts, setAlerts] = useState<FraudAlert[]>([]);
    86   const [auditLogs, setAuditLogs] = useState<AuditLog[]>([]);
    87   const [alertsLoading, setAlertsLoading] = useState(true);
    88   const [logsLoading, setLogsLoading] = useState(true);
    89   const [alertFilter, setAlertFilter] = useState({ severity: 'all', reviewed: 'all' });
    90   const [logFilter, setLogFilter] = useState({ action: 'all', search: '' });
    91   const [detailAlert, setDetailAlert] = useState<FraudAlert | null>(null);
    92   const [detailLog, setDetailLog] = useState<AuditLog | null>(null);
    93   const [stats, setStats] = useState({ total: 0, high: 0, unreviewed: 0, todayLogs: 0 });
    94 
    95   const loadAlerts = useCallback(async () => {
    96     setAlertsLoading(true);
    97     const { data } = await supabase
    98       .from('fraud_alerts')
    99       .select('*')
   100       .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
   101       .limit(200);
   102     const arr = Array.isArray(data) ? data : [];
   103     setAlerts(arr);
   104     setStats(s => ({
   105       ...s,
   106       total: arr.length,
   107       high: arr.filter(a => a.severity === 'high').length,
   108       unreviewed: arr.filter(a => !a.is_reviewed).length,
   109     }));
   110     setAlertsLoading(false);
   111   }, []);
   112 
   113   const loadLogs = useCallback(async () => {
   114     setLogsLoading(true);
   115     const { data } = await supabase
   116       .from('audit_logs')
   117       .select('*')
   118       .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
   119       .limit(500);
   120     const arr = Array.isArray(data) ? data : [];
   121     setAuditLogs(arr);
   122     const today = new Date().toDateString();
   123     setStats(s => ({
   124       ...s,
   125       todayLogs: arr.filter(l => new Date(l.created_at).toDateString() === today).length,
   126     }));
   127     setLogsLoading(false);
   128   }, []);
   129 
   130   useEffect(() => {
   131     loadAlerts();
   132     loadLogs();
   133 
   134     // Realtime subscription for fraud_alerts
   135     const channel = supabase
   136       .channel('fraud-realtime')
   137       .on('postgres_changes', { event: 'INSERT', schema: 'public', table: 'fraud_alerts' }, async (payload) => {
   138         const newAlert = payload.new as FraudAlert;
   139         setAlerts(prev => [newAlert, ...prev]);
   140         toast.warning('⚠️ พบพฤติกรรมน่าสงสัยใหม่!', { duration: 5000 });
   141 
   142         // ส่ง Telegram แจ้งเตือนทันที
   143         try {
   144           const { data: storeSettings } = await supabase
   145             .from('store_settings')
   146             .select('telegram_bot_token, telegram_chat_id, store_name')
   147             .maybeSingle();
   148           if (storeSettings?.telegram_bot_token && storeSettings?.telegram_chat_id) {
   149             const severityIcon = newAlert.severity === 'high' ? '🚨' : newAlert.severity === 'medium' ? '⚠️' : 'ℹ️';

    32 type PresetKey = 'today' | 'yesterday' | 'week' | 'month' | 'custom';
    33 
    34 function toDateStr(d: Date) { return d.toISOString().split('T')[0]; }
    35 
    36 function getPresetRange(key: PresetKey): { from: string; to: string } {
    37   const now = new Date();
    38   const today = toDateStr(now);
    39   if (key === 'today') return { from: today, to: today };
    40   if (key === 'yesterday') {
    41     const y = new Date(now); y.setDate(now.getDate() - 1);
    42     const ys = toDateStr(y); return { from: ys, to: ys };
    43   }
    44   if (key === 'week') {
    45     const w = new Date(now); w.setDate(now.getDate() - 6);
    46     return { from: toDateStr(w), to: today };
    47   }
    48   if (key === 'month') {
    49     return { from: `${now.getFullYear()}-${String(now.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-01`, to: today };
    50   }
    51   return { from: today, to: today };
    52 }

   110   const [summary, setSummary] = useState<SalesSummary | null>(null);
   111   const [chartData, setChartData] = useState<ChartPoint[]>([]);

   113   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
   114 
   115   const getRange = useCallback(() => {
   116     if (preset === 'custom') return { from: customFrom, to: customTo };
   117     return getPresetRange(preset);
   118   }, [preset, customFrom, customTo]);
   119 
   120   const loadReport = useCallback(async () => {
   121     setLoading(true);
   122     const { from, to } = getRange();
   123 
   124     const { data: txData } = await supabase
   125       .from('transactions')
   126       .select('total, created_at, items:transaction_items(product_name, quantity, unit_price, cost, subtotal)')
   127       .gte('created_at', `${from}T00:00:00`)
   128       .lte('created_at', `${to}T23:59:59`)
   129       .eq('status', 'completed')
   130       .order('created_at');
   131 
   132     const txArr = Array.isArray(txData) ? txData : [];
   133     const totalSales = txArr.reduce((s: number, t: any) => s + (t.total || 0), 0);
   134     const totalOrders = txArr.length;
   135     const totalProfit = txArr.reduce((s: number, t: any) =>
   136       s + (Array.isArray(t.items) ? t.items : []).reduce((si: number, i: any) => si + ((i.unit_price - i.cost) * i.quantity), 0), 0);
   137     const profitMargin = totalSales > 0 ? (totalProfit / totalSales) * 100 : 0;
   138     const avgOrderValue = totalOrders > 0 ? totalSales / totalOrders : 0;
   139     setSummary({ totalSales, totalOrders, totalProfit, profitMargin, avgOrderValue });
   140 
   141     // Top products
   142     const productMap: Record<string, TopProduct> = {};
   143     txArr.forEach((t: any) => {
   144       (Array.isArray(t.items) ? t.items : []).forEach((i: any) => {
   145         if (!productMap[i.product_name]) productMap[i.product_name] = { name: i.product_name, qty: 0, revenue: 0 };
   146         productMap[i.product_name].qty += i.quantity;
   147         productMap[i.product_name].revenue += i.subtotal || (i.unit_price * i.quantity);
   148       });
   149     });
   150     setTopProducts(Object.values(productMap).sort((a, b) => b.qty - a.qty).slice(0, 10));
   151     setChartData(buildChartData(txArr, from, to));
   152     setLoading(false);
   153   }, [getRange]);
   154

   131 // ============ Zod schema ============
   132 const roleSchema = z.object({
   133   name: z.string().min(1, 'กรุณากรอกชื่อยศ').max(50, 'ชื่อยศยาวเกินไป'),
   134   color: z.string().min(4, 'กรุณาเลือกสี'),
   135   permissions: z.record(z.boolean()),
   136 });
   137 type RoleForm = z.infer<typeof roleSchema>;

   144 export default function RolesPage() {
   145   const { profile } = useAuth();
   146   const [roles, setRoles] = useState<Role[]>([]);
   147   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
   148   const [editingRole, setEditingRole] = useState<Role | null>(null);
   149   const [isCreateOpen, setIsCreateOpen] = useState(false);
   150   const [deleteTarget, setDeleteTarget] = useState<Role | null>(null);
   151   const [userCounts, setUserCounts] = useState<Record<string, number>>({});
   152   const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('roles');
   153 
   154   useEffect(() => { loadRoles(); }, []);
   155 
   156   const loadRoles = async () => {
   157     setLoading(true);
   158     const { data } = await supabase
   159       .from('roles')
   160       .select('*')
   161       .order('sort_order');
   162     setRoles(Array.isArray(data) ? data : []);
   163 
   164     // นับจำนวนผู้ใช้ต่อยศ
   165     const { data: profileData } = await supabase
   166       .from('profiles')
   167       .select('role_id')
   168       .not('role_id', 'is', null);
   169     const counts: Record<string, number> = {};
   170     (profileData || []).forEach((p: { role_id: string }) => {
   171       if (p.role_id) counts[p.role_id] = (counts[p.role_id] || 0) + 1;
   172     });
   173     setUserCounts(counts);
   174     setLoading(false);
   175   };
   176 
   177   const form = useForm<RoleForm>({
   178     resolver: zodResolver(roleSchema),
   179     defaultValues: {
   180       name: '',
   181       color: '#3B82F6',
   182       permissions: Object.fromEntries(ALL_PERMISSION_KEYS.map(k => [k, false])),
   183     },
   184   });
   185 
   186   const openCreate = (template?: RoleTemplate) => {
   187     form.reset({
   188       name: template ? template.name + ' (คัดลอก)' : '',
   189       color: template?.color ?? '#3B82F6',
   190       permissions: Object.fromEntries(
   191         ALL_PERMISSION_KEYS.map(k => [k, template?.permissions[k] ?? false])
   192       ),
   193     });
   194     setEditingRole(null);
   195     setIsCreateOpen(true);
   196   };
   197 
   198   const openEdit = (role: Role) => {
   199     form.reset({
   200       name: role.name,
   201       color: role.color,
   202       permissions: Object.fromEntries(
   203         ALL_PERMISSION_KEYS.map(k => [k, role.permissions[k] ?? false])
   204       ),
   205     });
   206     setEditingRole(role);
   207     setIsCreateOpen(true);
   208   };
   209 
   210   const handleSave = async (values: RoleForm) => {
   211     if (editingRole) {
   212       const { error } = await supabase
   213         .from('roles')
   214         .update({ name: values.name, color: values.color, permissions: values.permissions, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() })
   215         .eq('id', editingRole.id);
   216       if (error) { toast.error('แก้ไขยศไม่สำเร็จ: ' + error.message); return; }
   217       toast.success('แก้ไขยศเรียบร้อย');
   218     } else {
   219       const { error } = await supabase
   220         .from('roles')
   221         .insert({ name: values.name, color: values.color, permissions: values.permissions, store_id: profile?.store_id ?? null });
   222       if (error) { toast.error('สร้างยศไม่สำเร็จ: ' + error.message); return; }
   223       toast.success('สร้างยศใหม่เรียบร้อย');
   224     }
   225     setIsCreateOpen(false);
   226     loadRoles();
   227   };
   228 
   229   const handleDelete = async () => {
   230     if (!deleteTarget) return;
   231     if ((userCounts[deleteTarget.id] || 0) > 0) {
   232       toast.error('ไม่สามารถลบยศที่มีพนักงานอยู่ได้ กรุณาเปลี่ยนยศพนักงานก่อน');
   233       setDeleteTarget(null);
   234       return;
   235     }
   236     const { error } = await supabase.from('roles').delete().eq('id', deleteTarget.id);
   237     if (error) { toast.error('ลบยศไม่สำเร็จ: ' + error.message); return; }
   238     toast.success('ลบยศเรียบร้อย');
   239     setDeleteTarget(null);
   240     loadRoles();
   241   };
   242 
   243   const toggleAllInGroup = (groupKeys: PermissionKey[], enabled: boolean) => {
   244     const current = form.getValues('permissions') as Record<string, boolean>;
   245     groupKeys.forEach(k => { current[k] = enabled; });
   246     form.setValue('permissions', current, { shouldDirty: true });
   247   };
   248 
   249   const permissionValues = form.watch('permissions') as Record<string, boolean>;

   251   return (

   253       {/* Header */}
   254       <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-4 flex-wrap">
   255         <div>

   137       .channel('fraud-realtime')
   138       .on('postgres_changes', { event: 'INSERT', schema: 'public', table: 'fraud_alerts' }, async (payload) => {
   139         const newAlert = payload.new as FraudAlert;
   140         setAlerts(prev => [newAlert, ...prev]);

   182     if (alertFilter.reviewed === 'unreviewed' && a.is_reviewed) return false;
   183     if (alertFilter.reviewed === 'reviewed' && !a.is_reviewed) return false;
   184     return true;
   185   });
   186 
   187   // Filter logs
